[30;1m1447 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m1448 | [0m[35mUnder the hood, the `run` function calls `pytest.main` to start the test[0m
[30;1m1449 | [0m[35mrun, and will pass the return code back to the caller. At the time of[0m
[30;1m1450 | [0m[35mwriting, this means it will return a `0` if all tests are successful,[0m

[30;1m1403 | [0m[35m## Using the run() function[0m
[30;1m1404 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m1405 | [0m[35mBecause the `run()` function (see [examples](/examples)) calls directly into the[0m

[30;1m578 | [0m[35m'Strict' key checking can be enabled or disabled globally, per test, or per[0m
[30;1m579 | [0m[35mstage. 'Strict' key checking refers to whether extra keys in the response should[0m
